CORRECTION *By authors*.The production cross sections are         O083300100040 
           calculated by applying several corrections-            O083300100041 
           the measured dead-time of the data-acquisition         O083300100042 
           system, the efficiency of the detection system, the    O083300100043 
           correction for non-fully stripped ions, correction for O083300100044 
           secondary reactions in the FRS beam line, correction   O083300100045 
           for angular transmission, correction for secondary     O083300100046 
           reactions inside the target.                           O083300100047 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) the systematic error on the production cross   O083300100048 
           sections due to uncertainties of all the above         O083300100049 
           mentioned corrections was estimated to Be 15% for all  O083300100050 
           fission fragments. For spallation residues a final     O083300100051 
           systematic error ranging from of 9% for lead to 25%    O083300100052 
           for promethium was estimated.                          O083300100053
